# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
So 
9*4
12*3
18*2 are just repeating itself 

but if we find a way to only calculate the 
from which count do we need to choose number 
it would take less time complexity 
 ^KW22vDEE

Advance approach :
now we only checking 2,3,4,5,6
but as we know every multiple of 2
is not prime because it divide by 2 , ^oarNCUEn

```java
boolean[] isPrime = new boolean[n+1];           
Arrays.fill(isPrime, true);                     
isPrime[0] = isPrime[1] = false;                

for(int i=2; i*i<=n; i++) {                    
    if(isPrime[i]) {                            
        for(int j=i*i; j<=n; j+=i) {           
            isPrime[j] = false;                
        }
    }
} ^valmod1F

Each time we get a multiple it means it must be a non prime so we do isPrime[j]=false ^vzD7qBQM

It means i iterate 1 to 5 only 
but it is outer loop so 
when i=1 j move till j<=n ^04GKZMt5

j=4 when i=2 ^QNuTy49G

j=9 when i=3
but 9 is out of bound j<=n ^YLyRM9AS

Same with 4 and 6 ^Kh3SoTfP

the 4 must be false 
and hench in the end True marked as Prime and 
non prime marked as False ^fdUQb8Td
